# Invasive Weed algorithm

#### Based on fitness function to evaluate seed coordinates (x and y)
```
fitness = x * sin(4*x) ) + ( 1.1 * y * sin( 2 * y)
>>        where 0 < x < 10 and 0 < y < 10
```
#### Find the best seed coordinates (minimum fitness)

}

  -ms-filter: "progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.BasicImage(rotation=2)";

  transform: rotate(180deg);
}
.fa-rotate-270 {
  -ms-filter: "progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.BasicImage(rotation=3)";
  -webkit-transform: rotate(270deg);

  transform: rotate(270deg);
}
.fa-flip-horizontal {
  -ms-filter: "progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.BasicImage(rotation=0, mirror=1)";
  -webkit-transform: scale(-1, 1);
  -ms-transform: scale(-1, 1);
  transform: scale(-1, 1);
}
.fa-flip-vertical {
  -ms-filter: "progid:DXImageTransform.Microsoft.BasicImage(rotation=2, mirror=1)";
  -webkit-transform: scale(1, -1);
  -ms-transform: scale(1, -1);
  transform: scale(1, -1);
}

/* Flexible box model classes */
/* Taken from Alex Russell http://infrequently.org/2009/08/css-3-progress/ */
/* This file is a compatability layer.  It allows the usage of flexible box 
model layouts accross multiple browsers, including older browsers.  The newest,
universal implementation of the flexible box model is used when available (see
`Modern browsers` comments below).  Browsers that are known to implement this 
new spec completely include:

    Firefox 28.0+
    Chrome 29.0+
    Internet Explorer 11+ 
    Opera 17.0+

Browsers not listed, including Safari, are supported via the styling under the
`Old browsers` comments below.
*/
.hbox {
  /* Old browsers */
  display: -webkit-box;
  -webkit-box-orient: horizontal;
  -webkit-box-align: stretch;
  display: -moz-box;
  -moz-box-orient: horizontal;
  -moz-box-align: stretch;
  display: box;
  box-orient: horizontal;
  box-align: stretch;
  /* Modern browsers */
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: row;
  align-items: stretch;
}
.hbox > * {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-flex: 0;
  -moz-box-flex: 0;
  box-flex: 0;
  /* Modern browsers */
  flex: none;
}
.vbox {
  /* Old browsers */
  display: -webkit-box;
  -webkit-box-orient: vertical;
  -webkit-box-align: stretch;
  display: -moz-box;
  -moz-box-orient: vertical;
  -moz-box-align: stretch;
  display: box;
  box-orient: vertical;
  box-align: stretch;
  /* Modern browsers */
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  align-items: stretch;
}
.vbox > * {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-flex: 0;
  -moz-box-flex: 0;
  box-flex: 0;
  /* Modern browsers */
  flex: none;
}
.hbox.reverse,
.vbox.reverse,
.reverse {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-direction: reverse;
  -moz-box-direction: reverse;
  box-direction: reverse;
  /* Modern browsers */
  flex-direction: row-reverse;
}
.hbox.box-flex0,
.vbox.box-flex0,
.box-flex0 {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-flex: 0;
  -moz-box-flex: 0;
  box-flex: 0;
  /* Modern browsers */
  flex: none;
  width: auto;
}
.hbox.box-flex1,
.vbox.box-flex1,
.box-flex1 {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-flex: 1;
  -moz-box-flex: 1;
  box-flex: 1;
  /* Modern browsers */
  flex: 1;
}
.hbox.box-flex,
.vbox.box-flex,
.box-flex {
  /* Old browsers */
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-flex: 1;
  -moz-box-flex: 1;
  box-flex: 1;
  /* Modern browsers */
  flex: 1;
}
.hbox.box-flex2,
.vbox.box-flex2,
.box-flex2 {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-flex: 2;
  -moz-box-flex: 2;
  box-flex: 2;
  /* Modern browsers */
  flex: 2;
}
.box-group1 {
  /*  Deprecated */
  -webkit-box-flex-group: 1;
  -moz-box-flex-group: 1;
  box-flex-group: 1;
}
.box-group2 {
  /* Deprecated */
  -webkit-box-flex-group: 2;
  -moz-box-flex-group: 2;
  box-flex-group: 2;
}
.hbox.start,
.vbox.start,
.start {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-pack: start;
  -moz-box-pack: start;
  box-pack: start;
  /* Modern browsers */
  justify-content: flex-start;
}
.hbox.end,
.vbox.end,
.end {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-pack: end;
  -moz-box-pack: end;
  box-pack: end;
  /* Modern browsers */
  justify-content: flex-end;
}
.hbox.center,
.vbox.center,
.center {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-pack: center;
  -moz-box-pack: center;
  box-pack: center;
  /* Modern browsers */
  justify-content: center;
}
.hbox.baseline,
.vbox.baseline,
.baseline {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-pack: baseline;
  -moz-box-pack: baseline;
  box-pack: baseline;
  /* Modern browsers */
  justify-content: baseline;
}
.hbox.stretch,
.vbox.stretch,
.stretch {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-pack: stretch;
  -moz-box-pack: stretch;
  box-pack: stretch;
  /* Modern browsers */
  justify-content: stretch;
}
.hbox.align-start,
.vbox.align-start,
.align-start {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-align: start;
  -moz-box-align: start;
  box-align: start;
  /* Modern browsers */
  align-items: flex-start;
}
.hbox.align-end,
.vbox.align-end,
.align-end {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-align: end;
  -moz-box-align: end;
  box-align: end;
  /* Modern browsers */
  align-items: flex-end;
}
.hbox.align-center,
.vbox.align-center,
.align-center {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-align: center;
  -moz-box-align: center;
  box-align: center;
  /* Modern browsers */
  align-items: center;
}
.hbox.align-baseline,
.vbox.align-baseline,
.align-baseline {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-align: baseline;
  -moz-box-align: baseline;
  box-align: baseline;
  /* Modern browsers */
  align-items: baseline;
}
.hbox.align-stretch,
.vbox.align-stretch,
.align-stretch {
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-align: stretch;
  -moz-box-align: stretch;
  box-align: stretch;
  /* Modern browsers */
  align-items: stretch;
}

div.cell {
  /* Old browsers */
  display: -webkit-box;
  -webkit-box-orient: vertical;
  -webkit-box-align: stretch;
  display: -moz-box;
  -moz-box-orient: vertical;
  -moz-box-align: stretch;
  display: box;
  box-orient: vertical;
  box-align: stretch;
  /* Modern browsers */
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  align-items: stretch;
  border-radius: 2px;
  box-sizing: border-box;
  -moz-box-sizing: border-box;
  -webkit-box-sizing: border-box;
  border-width: 1px;
  border-style: solid;
  border-color: transparent;
  width: 100%;
  padding: 5px;
  /* This acts as a spacer between cells, that is outside the border */
  margin: 0px;
  outline: none;
  position: relative;
  overflow: visible;
}
div.cell:before {
  position: absolute;
  display: block;
  top: -1px;
  left: -1px;
  width: 5px;
  height: calc(100% +  2px);
  content: '';
  background: transparent;
}

  border-right-width: 1px;
  background: #E3F2FD;

.prompt {
  /* This needs to be wide enough for 3 digit prompt numbers: In[100]: */
  min-width: 14ex;
  /* This padding is tuned to match the padding on the CodeMirror editor. */
  padding: 0.4em;
  margin: 0px;
  font-family: monospace;
  text-align: right;
  /* This has to match that of the the CodeMirror class line-height below */
  line-height: 1.21429em;
  /* Don't highlight prompt number selection */
  -webkit-touch-callout: none;
  -webkit-user-select: none;
  -khtml-user-select: none;
  -moz-user-select: none;
  -ms-user-select: none;
  user-select: none;
  /* Use default cursor */
  cursor: default;
}
@media (max-width: 540px) {
  .prompt {
    text-align: left;
  }
}

  min-width: 0;
  /* Old browsers */
  display: -webkit-box;

  display: -moz-box;
  -moz-box-orient: vertical;
  -moz-box-align: stretch;
  display: box;
  box-orient: vertical;
  box-align: stretch;
  /* Modern browsers */
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  align-items: stretch;
  /* Old browsers */
  -webkit-box-flex: 1;
  -moz-box-flex: 1;
  box-flex: 1;
  /* Modern browsers */
  flex: 1;
}

   is no content in the output_subarea and the prompt. The main purpose of this is
   to make sure that empty JavaScript output_subareas have no height. */

  padding-top: 0;
  padding-bottom: 0;
}

/* The following gets added to the <head> if it is detected that the user has a
 * monospace font with inconsistent normal/bold/italic height.  See
 * notebookmain.js.  Such fonts will have keywords vertically offset with
 * respect to the rest of the text.  The user should select a better font.
 * See: https://github.com/ipython/ipython/issues/1503
 *
 * .CodeMirror span {
 *      vertical-align: bottom;
 * }
 */
.CodeMirror {
  line-height: 1.21429em;
  /* Changed from 1em to our global default */
  font-size: 14px;
  height: auto;
  /* Changed to auto to autogrow */
  background: none;
  /* Changed from white to allow our bg to show through */
}
.CodeMirror-scroll {
  /*  The CodeMirror docs are a bit fuzzy on if overflow-y should be hidden or visible.*/
  /*  We have found that if it is visible, vertical scrollbars appear with font size changes.*/
  overflow-y: hidden;
  overflow-x: auto;
}
.CodeMirror-lines {
  /* In CM2, this used to be 0.4em, but in CM3 it went to 4px. We need the em value because */
  /* we have set a different line-height and want this to scale with that. */
  /* Note that this should set vertical padding only, since CodeMirror assumes
       that horizontal padding will be set on CodeMirror pre */
  padding: 0.4em 0;
}
.CodeMirror-linenumber {
  padding: 0 8px 0 4px;
}
.CodeMirror-gutters {
  border-bottom-left-radius: 2px;
  border-top-left-radius: 2px;
}
.CodeMirror pre {
  /* In CM3 this went to 4px from 0 in CM2. This sets horizontal padding only,
    use .CodeMirror-lines for vertical */
  padding: 0 0.4em;
  border: 0;
  border-radius: 0;
}
.CodeMirror-cursor {
  border-left: 1.4px solid black;
}
@media screen and (min-width: 2138px) and (max-width: 4319px) {
  .CodeMirror-cursor {
    border-left: 2px solid black;
  }
}
@media screen and (min-width: 4320px) {
  .CodeMirror-cursor {
    border-left: 4px solid black;
  }
}

  <div tabindex="-1" id="notebook" class="border-box-sizing">

<div class="cell border-box-sizing text_cell rendered"><div class="prompt input_prompt">
</div><div class="inner_cell">
<div class="text_cell_render border-box-sizing rendered_html">
<h1 id="Invasive-Weed-algorithm">Invasive Weed algorithm<a class="anchor-link" href="#Invasive-Weed-algorithm">&#182;</a></h1><p><br></p>
<h3 id="Based-on-fitness-function-to-evaluate-seed-coordinates-(x-and-y)">Based on fitness function to evaluate seed coordinates (x and y)<a class="anchor-link" href="#Based-on-fitness-function-to-evaluate-seed-coordinates-(x-and-y)">&#182;</a></h3>
<pre><code>fitness = x * sin(4*x) ) + ( 1.1 * y * sin( 2 * y)
        where 0 &lt; x &lt; 10 and 0 &lt; y &lt; 10</code></pre>
<h3 id="Find-the-best-seed-coordinates-(minimum-fitness)">Find the best seed coordinates (minimum fitness)<a class="anchor-link" href="#Find-the-best-seed-coordinates-(minimum-fitness)">&#182;</a></h3>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[106]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="c1"># Import necessary libraries</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">numpy</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="nn">np</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">random</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">math</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">collections</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">operator</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">time</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">progressbar</span>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="nn">matplotlib.pyplot</span> <span class="k">as</span> <span class="nn">plt</span>
</pre></div>

<div class="cell border-box-sizing code_cell rendered">
<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[107]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="k">class</span> <span class="nc">InvasiveWeed</span><span class="p">():</span> <span class="c1"># Define class with model name</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="fm">__init__</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">pmax</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">maxiter</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">delta_cap</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">num_exceeded_delta</span><span class="p">):</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate class with required parameters</span>
        <span class="n">seed_array</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate empty list to contain tuples of x and y seed coordinates</span>
        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="nb">range</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">round</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mf">0.1</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">pmax</span><span class="p">)):</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate 10% of population max seeds with random x and y values between 0 and 10</span>
            <span class="n">x</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">random</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">uniform</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1"># x = random float between 0 and 10</span>
            <span class="n">y</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">random</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">uniform</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1"># y = random fload between 0 and 10</span>
            <span class="c1"># Append the seed to the seed_array</span>
            <span class="n">seed_array</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">append</span><span class="p">((</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="p">))</span> 

        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">pmax</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">pmax</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">maxiter</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">maxiter</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">delta_cap</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">delta_cap</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">num_exceeded_delta</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">num_exceeded_delta</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># Initiate delta higher than delta_cap to avoid early iteration stoppage</span>
        <span class="n">delta</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">delta_cap</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mf">0.01</span>
        
        <span class="n">c</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate int c for num_xceed_delta count</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># current_fitness_dict will contain the seed coordinates and their fitness scores</span>
        <span class="c1"># for all seeds in our current population (capped to pmax)</span>
        <span class="n">current_fitness_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{}</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">current_fitness_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">current_fitness_dict</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># Initiate list that will contain best fitness score from each iteration</span>
        <span class="n">best_fitness_list</span> <span class="o">=</span>  <span class="p">[]</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">best_fitness_list</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">best_fitness_list</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># Initiate list that will contain best scoring seeds from each iteration</span>
        <span class="n">best_seed_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{}</span>
        <span class="n">best_seed_list</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">best_seed_list</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">best_seed_list</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">best_seed_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">best_seed_dict</span>

        <span class="c1"># Get the time in seconds to count the runtime of the loop        </span>
        <span class="n">start_time</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">time</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">time</span><span class="p">()</span> 

        
        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="nb">range</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">maxiter</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">):</span> <span class="c1"># Iterate n = maxiter times</span>
            <span class="n">fitness_array</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">get_fitness</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">seed_array</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1"># Get fitness array for current seeds</span>
            <span class="n">fitness_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">dict</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">zip</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">seed_array</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">fitness_array</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="c1"># Make a dictionary containing seed tuple as key and their fitness as values</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Sort seed --&gt; fitness dictionary</span>
            <span class="c1"># The lowest scoring fitness value first (the best score)</span>
            <span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="n">k</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">v</span> <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">k</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">v</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="nb">sorted</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">(),</span> <span class="n">key</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="k">lambda</span> <span class="n">item</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">item</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">])}</span> 
            <span class="n">best_seed_dict</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">keys</span><span class="p">())[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">values</span><span class="p">())[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span>
            <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">best_seed_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">best_seed_dict</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Append best seed to global list</span>
            <span class="n">best_seed_list</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">append</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">values</span><span class="p">())[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">])</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Normalize fitness value in the dictionary</span>
            <span class="c1"># Increase the distribution of fitness scores so they start with 0 instead of negative values</span>
            <span class="n">normalized_fitness_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">normalize_fitness</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span><span class="p">)</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Compute number of children to be made from each seed</span>
            <span class="c1"># and output as a new directory with seed as key and number of children as values</span>
            <span class="n">seed_children_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">eval_fitness</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">normalized_fitness_dict</span><span class="p">)</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Append best fitness score to the global fitness_array</span>
            <span class="n">best_fitness_list</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">append</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">sorted</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">fitness_array</span><span class="p">)[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">])</span>
            <span class="c1">#print(best_fitness_list,&quot;\n&quot;)</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Add seeds and their fitness scores from this iteration to the population (current_fitness_dict)</span>
            <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">seed</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">fitness</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">():</span>
                <span class="n">current_fitness_dict</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">seed</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">fitness</span>

            
            <span class="c1"># If population is bigger than the set pmax</span>
            <span class="c1"># we need to trim it by keeping only best scoring seeds</span>
            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">current_fitness_dict</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="n">pmax</span><span class="p">:</span>
                    <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">prune_seeds</span><span class="p">()</span>

            
            <span class="c1"># Generate new seeds and add them to current array of seeds</span>
            <span class="n">seed_array</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">seed_array</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">generate_population</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">seed_children_dict</span><span class="p">)</span>

            <span class="c1"># After 5 iterations (minimum),</span>
            <span class="c1"># Start checking whether the delta (difference between last and second last fitness scores)</span>
            <span class="c1"># is higher than the cap on the score difference set by the user as delta_cap</span>
            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">best_seed_dict</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="mi">5</span><span class="p">:</span>
                <span class="c1"># Subtract best fitness from the last two iterations </span>
                <span class="n">delta</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">best_fitness_list</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="n">best_fitness_list</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">]</span>
            <span class="k">else</span><span class="p">:</span>
                <span class="c1"># Before 5 iterations the fitness has been very variable and could produce an error with a 0 delta</span>
                <span class="c1"># we avoid it by adding 0.01 to the delta to avoid this</span>
                <span class="n">delta</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">delta_cap</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mf">0.01</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># If delta is lower than the delta_cap set bby user</span>
            <span class="c1"># add to the counter for threshold of num_exceeded_data</span>
            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">delta</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="n">delta_cap</span><span class="p">:</span>
                <span class="n">c</span> <span class="o">+=</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Otherwise set the counter back to 0</span>
            <span class="k">else</span><span class="p">:</span>
                <span class="n">c</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span>

            <span class="c1"># Break the function if the delta has been lower than the delta_cap</span>
            <span class="c1"># more than the num_exceeded_data set by the user</span>
            <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">c</span> <span class="o">&gt;=</span> <span class="n">num_exceeded_delta</span><span class="p">:</span>
                <span class="k">break</span>
            
                
            <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="c1"># Keep track of the last iteration</span>

            

        <span class="n">end_time</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">time</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">time</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="c1"># Get time in seconds</span>
        <span class="n">runtime</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">end_time</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="n">start_time</span> <span class="c1"># Get runtime of the model</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">runtime</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">runtime</span> <span class="c1"># Make runtime accessable inside the class</span>
    
    
    <span class="c1"># Function to generate the new seeds in each generation</span>
    <span class="c1"># Based on their previous fitness</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">generate_population</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">seed_children_dict</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="n">new_seeds</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate list of new seeds</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># Based on how many new children each previous fitness parent produces</span>
        <span class="c1"># Inititate new seeds within 0.1 standard distributions from previous parent coordinates</span>
        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">seed</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">nchildren</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">seed_children_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">():</span>
            <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">_</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="nb">range</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">nchildren</span><span class="p">):</span> <span class="c1"># this loop will run as long as nchildren for each parent</span>
                <span class="n">x</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">seed</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="c1"># X coordinate</span>
                <span class="n">y</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">seed</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="c1"># Y coordinate</span>
                <span class="n">new_x</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">random</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">gauss</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mf">0.1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate new x</span>
                <span class="n">new_y</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">random</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">gauss</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mf">0.1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate new y</span>

                <span class="c1"># If x was outside set bounds (0,10), Initiate new x until a correct one is produced</span>
                <span class="k">while</span> <span class="n">new_x</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="ow">or</span> <span class="n">new_x</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">:</span>
                    <span class="n">new_x</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">random</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">gauss</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mf">0.1</span><span class="p">)</span>

                <span class="c1"># If y was outside set bounds (0,10), Initiate new y until a correct one is produced</span>
                <span class="k">while</span> <span class="n">new_y</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="ow">or</span> <span class="n">new_y</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">:</span>
                    <span class="n">new_y</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">random</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">gauss</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mf">0.1</span><span class="p">)</span>

                <span class="c1"># Append new seeds to the population</span>
                <span class="n">new_seeds</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">append</span><span class="p">((</span><span class="n">new_x</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">new_y</span><span class="p">))</span>

        <span class="c1"># Return new seeds from the function</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">new_seeds</span>
    
    <span class="c1"># Get fitness of new seeds</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">get_fitness</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">seed_array</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="n">fitness_array</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate fitness array for new seeds</span>
        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">seed</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">seed_array</span><span class="p">:</span>
            <span class="n">x</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">seed</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="c1">#  X coordinate</span>
            <span class="n">y</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">seed</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="c1">#  Y coordinate</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Functon to convert x and y coordinates into a fitness value</span>
            <span class="n">fitness</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">x</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">math</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">sin</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="p">(</span> <span class="mf">1.1</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">y</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">math</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">sin</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="mi">2</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">y</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">)</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Append fitness to the fitness array</span>
            <span class="n">fitness_array</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">append</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">fitness</span><span class="p">)</span>
            
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">fitness_array</span>
    
    
    <span class="c1"># Function to normalize fitness into values from 0 to max</span>
    <span class="c1"># Slide the values to positives based on the lowest negative values</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">normalize_fitness</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="c1"># Get the seed with the best/lowest fitness</span>
        <span class="n">lowest_fitness_element</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">())[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span>
        
        <span class="n">new_vals</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate list for new fitness values</span>
        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">val</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">values</span><span class="p">():</span>
             <span class="c1"># Subtract value from the lowest value in sorted fitness dictionary</span>
            <span class="n">new_val</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">val</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">values</span><span class="p">())[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span>
            <span class="n">new_vals</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">append</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">new_val</span><span class="p">)</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># Save sorted dictionary with new values of fitness</span>
        <span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">dict</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">zip</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">keys</span><span class="p">(),</span> <span class="n">new_vals</span><span class="p">))</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># Keep the lowest fitness element to be accessed</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">lowest_fitness_element</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">lowest_fitness_element</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">sorted_fitness_dict</span>

    <span class="c1"># Generate variable number of seeds based on the fitness score of the parent seed</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">eval_fitness</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">normalized_fitness_dict</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="n">children_seed_list</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate list for new seeds number</span>
        <span class="n">maximum</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">max</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">normalized_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">values</span><span class="p">())</span> <span class="c1"># get maximum fitness value</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># Perform fitness to N children transformation based on each fitness value</span>
        <span class="c1"># and the maximum fitness value from this generation</span>
        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">val</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">normalized_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">values</span><span class="p">():</span> 
            <span class="c1"># (val+0.00001) makes sure that the 0 error does not occur</span>
            <span class="c1"># Other calculations were attempted but this one proved the most efficient for the task</span>
            <span class="n">num_seed</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">round</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="p">(</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">val</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mf">0.000001</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">/</span> <span class="n">maximum</span><span class="p">)</span>
            
            <span class="c1"># Append the num of new children to the pre-initialized list</span>
            <span class="n">children_seed_list</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">append</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">num_seed</span><span class="p">)</span>

        <span class="c1"># Create dictionary containing seeds and reversed number of children</span>
        <span class="c1"># That is because the lowest fitness score is one that should actually have most children</span>
        <span class="n">seed_children_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">dict</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">zip</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">normalized_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">keys</span><span class="p">(),</span> <span class="n">children_seed_list</span><span class="p">[::</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]))</span>

        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">seed_children_dict</span>

    <span class="c1"># Function to prune the seeds to the number of population maximum (pmax)</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">prune_seeds</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="c1"># Sort the current dictionary with seeds and their fitness based on fitness</span>
        <span class="n">sorted_current_fitness_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="n">k</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">v</span> <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">k</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">v</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="nb">sorted</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">current_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">(),</span> <span class="n">key</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="k">lambda</span> <span class="n">item</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">item</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">])}</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># Prune the sorted dictionary to population max (pmax) and return as class fitness dictionary</span>
        <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">current_fitness_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">dict</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_current_fitness_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">())[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">pmax</span><span class="p">])</span> 
    
    <span class="c1"># Return best iteration from class</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">return_best_iteration_</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">i</span>
    
    <span class="c1"># Return model runtime from class</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">return_runtime_</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">runtime</span>
    
    <span class="c1"># Return best seed from class</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">return_best_seed_</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="c1"># Make sure the current best fitness is the minimum of fitness values from the iterations</span>
        <span class="n">best_seed_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="n">k</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">v</span> <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">k</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">v</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="nb">sorted</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">best_seed_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">(),</span> <span class="n">key</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="k">lambda</span> <span class="n">item</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">item</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">])}</span>
        
        <span class="c1"># Return best seed</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">best_seed_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">(),</span> <span class="n">key</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="k">lambda</span> <span class="n">x</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">x</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]))</span>
    
    <span class="c1"># Return best fitness value from class</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">return_best_fitness_</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">best_seed_list</span><span class="p">)</span>
    
    <span class="c1"># Plot best fitness from each iteration/generation</span>
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">plot_fitnesses_</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">plot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">best_seed_list</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">title</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;Best fitness scores from each iteration/generation&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">show</span><span class="p">()</span>
    
    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="fm">__str__</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">):</span>
        <span class="k">return</span>  <span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;InvasiveWeed(pmax = </span><span class="si">{self.pmax}</span><span class="s2">, maxiter = </span><span class="si">{self.maxiter}</span><span class="s2">, delta_cap = </span><span class="si">{self.delta_cap}</span><span class="s2">, num_exceeded_delta = </span><span class="si">{self.num_exceeded_delta}</span><span class="s2">)</span><span class="se">\n</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span>
    
</pre></div>

    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="c1"># Perform grid search to find the best parameters based on the params dictionary</span>
<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">grid_search</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">params</span><span class="p">):</span>
    <span class="n">grid_search_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{}</span> <span class="c1"># Start dictionary for grid search results</span>
    <span class="n">runtimes</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span> <span class="c1"># Start list for runtimes for each time model runs</span>
    <span class="n">param_no</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">np</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">prod</span><span class="p">([</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">x</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">params</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">values</span><span class="p">()])</span> <span class="c1"># Compute number of totals iterations to run for the progress bar</span>
    <span class="n">total</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">progressbar</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">ProgressBar</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">maxval</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="n">param_no</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate progress bar</span>
    <span class="n">c</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate int c to update the progress bar</span>
    <span class="n">total</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">start</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="c1"># Start progress bar</span>
    <span class="n">best_seeds</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[]</span> <span class="c1"># Initiate list for best seeds from the entire grid search</span>
    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">pmax</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">params</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;pmax&#39;</span><span class="p">]:</span> <span class="c1"># For each population max value</span>
        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">maxiter</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">params</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;maxiter&#39;</span><span class="p">]:</span> <span class="c1"># For each max iteration value</span>
            <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">delta_cap</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">params</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;delta_cap&#39;</span><span class="p">]:</span> <span class="c1"># For each delta_cap value</span>
                <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">num_exceeded_delta</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">params</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;num_exceeded_delta&#39;</span><span class="p">]:</span> <span class="c1"># For each num exeeded delta value</span>
                    <span class="n">model</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">InvasiveWeed</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">pmax</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">maxiter</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">delta_cap</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">num_exceeded_delta</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1"># Iniiate model with current parameters</span>
                    <span class="n">best_fitness_score</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">model</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">return_best_fitness_</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="c1"># Get best fitness score from the model</span>
                    <span class="n">best_iteration</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">model</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">return_best_iteration_</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="c1"># Get best iteration from the model ( Should be last/highest one )\</span>
                    <span class="c1"># Update grid search dictionary with results</span>
                    <span class="n">grid_search_dict</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">pmax</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">maxiter</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">delta_cap</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">num_exceeded_delta</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">best_iteration</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">best_fitness_score</span> 
                    <span class="n">runtimes</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">append</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">model</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">return_runtime_</span><span class="p">())</span> <span class="c1"># Append runtime of current model to results dictionary</span>
                    <span class="n">best_seeds</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">append</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">model</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">return_best_seed_</span><span class="p">())</span> <span class="c1"># Append best seeds from best iteration from the model to the results dictionary</span>
                    <span class="n">total</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">update</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">c</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1"># Update progressbar with the int c value</span>
                    <span class="n">c</span><span class="o">+=</span><span class="mi">1</span> <span class="c1"># update int c value</span>
                    
                    
    <span class="n">total</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">finish</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="c1"># Finish progressbar</span>
    <span class="n">res_dic</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="n">k</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">v</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">k</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">v</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="n">grid_search_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">()}</span> <span class="c1"># res dict contains seed and minimum (best) fitness from each model run</span>
    <span class="n">sorted_results_dict</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="n">k</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">v</span> <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">k</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">v</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="nb">sorted</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">res_dic</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">items</span><span class="p">(),</span> <span class="n">key</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="k">lambda</span> <span class="n">item</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">item</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">])}</span>  <span class="c1"># Sort resulst dictionary</span>
    <span class="n">sorted_seeds</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">sorted</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">best_seeds</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">key</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="k">lambda</span> <span class="n">x</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">x</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">])</span> <span class="c1"># sort best seeds dictionary by fitness</span>
    
    <span class="n">best_params</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_results_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">keys</span><span class="p">())[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="c1"># Get params for best seed from gridsearch</span>
    <span class="n">best_fitness</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">sorted_results_dict</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">values</span><span class="p">())[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="c1"># Get best fitness from gridsearch</span>
    
    <span class="n">best_seed</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">sorted_seeds</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="c1"># Get best seed from gridsearch</span>
    
    <span class="n">best_round_fitnesses</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">list</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">grid_search_dict</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">best_params</span><span class="p">])</span> <span class="c1"># Get all fitnesses from the best model from gridsearch</span>
    
    <span class="c1"># Print the best model as well as the current best parameters</span>
    <span class="c1"># and best iteration, total runtime, best fitness and best seed from gridsearch</span>
    <span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="se">\n</span><span class="s2">Gridsearch results:&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="se">\t</span><span class="s2">Best model:&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="se">\t\t</span><span class="s2">InvasiveWeed(pmax = </span><span class="si">{best_params[0]}</span><span class="s2">, maxiter = </span><span class="si">{best_params[1]}</span><span class="s2">, delta_cap = </span><span class="si">{best_params[2]}</span><span class="s2">, num_exceeded_delta = </span><span class="si">{best_params[3]}</span><span class="s2">)</span><span class="se">\n</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="se">\t</span><span class="s2">Stopped at iteration: </span><span class="si">{best_params[4]}</span><span class="se">\n</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="se">\t</span><span class="s2">Total runtime: {round(sum(runtimes),3)} seconds</span><span class="se">\n</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="se">\t</span><span class="s2">Best fitness: </span><span class="si">{best_fitness}</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="se">\t</span><span class="s2">Best seed coordinates: </span><span class="si">{best_seed}</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
    
    <span class="c1"># Return best params, best fitness and all fitnesses from best round from the function</span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">best_params</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">best_fitness</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">best_round_fitnesses</span>
                
</pre></div>

<div class="input">
<div class="prompt input_prompt">In&nbsp;[109]:</div>
<div class="inner_cell">
    <div class="input_area">
<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="c1">## Grid search for the best seed (minimum fitness) with different parameters</span>

<span class="c1"># Dictionary with parameters to be run for gridsearch</span>
<span class="n">params</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="s1">&#39;pmax&#39;</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="o">**</span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="o">**</span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">2000</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="c1"># Population max variable</span>
    <span class="s1">&#39;maxiter&#39;</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">15</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">20</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="c1"># Max iteration variable</span>
    <span class="s1">&#39;delta_cap&#39;</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">10</span><span class="o">**-</span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="o">**-</span><span class="mi">8</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="c1"># Define the change to be accounted for in num_exceeded_delta</span>
    
    <span class="c1"># This variable defines how many times the difference between the fitness score of the last iteration versus</span>
    <span class="c1"># The second last iteration can exeed the value of delta_cap (the max delta value)</span>
    <span class="s1">&#39;num_exceeded_delta&#39;</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">8</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">10</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

<span class="c1"># Run gridsearch for parameters</span>
<span class="n">best_params</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">best_fitness</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">best_round_fitnesses</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">grid_search</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">params</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="c1"># plot best fitness score for each iteration in the best model from gridseach</span>
<span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">plot</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">best_round_fitnesses</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">title</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;Fitness scores from each iteration in the best model from gridseach&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="n">plt</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">show</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>

    </div>
</div>

<div class=" highlight hl-ipython3"><pre><span></span><span class="c1"># Check reliability of the model:</span>
<span class="c1"># Run model one single time with the best parameters from gridsearch</span>
<span class="c1"># The resulting best seed and fitness value should be similair to the gridsearch result</span>
<span class="c1"># Print model parameters, results and plot the fitness from each iteration</span>

<span class="n">model</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">InvasiveWeed</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">best_params</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="n">best_params</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="n">best_params</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="n">best_params</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">])</span>
<span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">&quot;Model: &quot;</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">model</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;Best iteration (stopped at): {model.return_best_iteration_()}&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;Model runtime: {model.return_runtime_()}</span><span class="se">\n</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;Best fitness: {min(model.return_best_fitness_())}&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>
<span class="nb">print</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="sa">f</span><span class="s2">&quot;Best seed: {model.return_best_seed_()[0]}</span><span class="se">\n</span><span class="s2">&quot;</span><span class="p">)</span>

<span class="n">model</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">plot_fitnesses_</span><span class="p">()</span>
</pre></div>
